   - The most popular game genres in Turkey are action (26%), shooter (22%), and sports (14%). (Source: Newzoo)
   
   - The number of mobile gamers in Turkey is estimated to reach 37.5 million in 2021, a 10% increase from 2019. (Source: Newzoo)
   
   - The average revenue per paying user (ARPPU) in the Turkish gaming market is $42. (Source: Newzoo)
   
   - The Turkish gaming market is expected to generate $1.6 billion in revenue in 2022, a 33% increase from 2019. (Source: Newzoo)
   
   - The most popular game titles in Turkey are PUBG Mobile, Fortnite, and Call of Duty: Mobile. (Source: SteamDB)
   
   - The number of esports enthusiasts in Turkey is estimated to reach 3.5 million in 2021, a 15% increase from 2019. (Source: Newzoo)
   
   - The Turkish gaming market is dominated by local game development studios, with TaleWorlds Entertainment, Peak Games, and Gram Games being the top three studios. (Source: Newzoo)
   
   - The Turkish gaming market is expected to grow at a compound annual growth rate (CAGR) of 14% from 2019 to 2024. (Source: Newzoo)
